PER_Iranian_elections_decision_category = {
	PER_auto_update_gui_weekly = {
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = { always = no }
		fire_only_once = no
		is_good = yes
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 7

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = PER }
				hidden_effect = {
					PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes
					if = { #8th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2001.6.1
								date < 2002.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.9
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.8
								days = 0
							}
						}

					}
					else_if = { #9th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2005.6.9
								date < 2006.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.11
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.10
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #10th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2009.6.5
								date < 2010.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.13
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.12
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #11th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2013.6.7
								date < 2014.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ghalibaf
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.15
									days = 0
								}
							}
							else = {
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.16
									days = 0
								}
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.14
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #12th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2017.5.12
								date < 2018.6.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.18
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.17
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #13th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2021.6.11
								date < 2022.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.20
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.19
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
						}
						activate_mission = PER_auto_update_gui_weekly
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

PER_soleimani = {
	PER_mount_international_pressure = {

		icon = decision_generic_civil_support

		visible = {
			original_tag = PER
		}

		cost = 20
		days_remove = 3
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_mount_international_pressure"
			add_political_power = 40
		}

		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = mount_international_pressure
			USA = {
				add_political_power = -50
				add_stability = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
	PER_complain_to_the_united_nations = {

		icon = decision_generic_decision

			original_tag = PER

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 15
		fire_only_once = yes

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_complain_to_the_united_nationss"
			add_war_support = 0.02
		}

		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = complain_to_the_united_nations

				add_political_power = -75
			}
		}
	}

		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {

	PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level = {

		icon = GFX_decision_fist

		days_remove = 5
		days_re_enable = 3
		cost = 200

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = PER_start_the_islamic_propaganda
			OR = {
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
			}

		}
		allowed = {
			original_tag = PER
		}
		available = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = PER_seda_o_sima_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_road_billboard_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_social_media_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_tehran_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_shiraz_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_mashhad_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_ahvaz_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_tabriz_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_isfahan_military_parade_decision
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = islamic_propaganda_status
						value = 100
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -5 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level_decision
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = islamic_propaganda_status
				value = 10
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
					add_idea = PER_unity_of_the_nation
				}
			}
			clear_variable = islamic_propaganda_status
			set_variable = { islamic_propaganda_status = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level_decision
		}
	}
}

		}

				}

			has_opinion = { target = SYR value > 9 }

				has_opinion = { target = PER value > 9 }
			}

				country_event = {
					id = axis_of_resistance_events.1
					days = 0
				}
			}

			base = 0

			}
		}
	}

			# Conservatives
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = PER_hashem_sabbaghian_minister

				has_country_flag = PER_mohammad_tavasoli_minister
				has_country_flag = PER_mostafa_moein_minister
				has_country_flag = PER_mostafa_tajzade_minister
			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = PER_presidential_decisions_only_one_is_available_TT
				NOT = {
					has_decision = PER_housing_projects
					has_decision = PER_appease_clerics
					has_decision = PER_rural_development
					has_decision = PER_regional_consolidation
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 90
		days_re_enable = 180

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_crack_down_on_crime"

		}
		modifier = {

	PER_start_the_revolution = {
		days_remove = 12
		fire_only_once = yes
		icon = generic_nationalism
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = PER_any_owned_state_has_militia_TT
				check_variable = { PER_state_modifier_var > 3 }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_start_the_revolution"
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { PER_state_modifier_var = 26 }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = PER_civilwar.1
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_civil_war_TT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { PER_state_modifier_var = 26 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = PER_civilwar.50
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = PER_civil_war_decision
			set_country_flag = PER_civil_war_decision_1
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { PER_state_modifier_var > 11 }
				add = 100
			}
		}
	}

			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PER_us_sanctions
				add_idea = PER_us_sanctions_harshened
			}
			clr_country_flag = PER_its_joever_nukes
			clr_country_flag = PER_nuclear_negotiations
		}
	}
}

PER_expose_iran = {
	expose_iranian_nuclear_program = {

		visible = {
			ROOT = {
				network_strength = {
					target = PER
					value > 89.99
				}
			}
			PER = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_nuclear_known
				}
				has_country_flag = PER_natanz_nuclear_facility
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout expose_iranian_nuclear_program"
			USA = {
				country_event = nuclear_iran.20
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = {
					id = PER_rev_flavor.20
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
